  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型是否具备连贯的内部世界模型仍是核心争议。传统下一令牌预测(NTP)关注单步监督，而多令牌预测(MTP)虽显示出学习结构化表征的潜力，但存在结构幻觉问题——离散令牌监督导致潜在空间中的非法捷径违反环境约束。因此需要一种方法既能利用MTP的优势，又能解决其幻觉问题，实现离散令牌与连续状态表征的有效对齐。

Method: 提出潜在语义增强MTP(LSE-MTP)方法，核心思想是将预测锚定到真实隐藏状态轨迹。具体通过梯度耦合机制诱导表征收缩性，使模型收敛到内部信念状态，同时避免离散令牌监督带来的结构幻觉问题。

Result: 在合成图和真实世界曼哈顿出租车乘车数据集上的实验表明，LSE-MTP有效弥合了离散令牌与连续状态表征之间的鸿沟，显著提升了表征对齐效果，减少了结构幻觉，并增强了对扰动的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: MTP相比NTP具有更优的归纳偏置，能促进内部世界模型的形成，但其结构幻觉问题需要通过LSE-MTP等方法进行潜在语义增强来解决。该研究为理解LLM内部表征学习提供了理论视角，并验证了通过轨迹锚定提升表征质量的有效性。

Abstract: Whether Large Language Models (LLMs) develop coherent internal world models remains a core debate. While conventional Next-Token Prediction (NTP) focuses on one-step-ahead supervision, Multi-Token Prediction (MTP) has shown promise in learning more structured representations. In this work, we provide a theoretical perspective analyzing the gradient inductive bias of MTP, supported by empirical evidence, showing that MTP promotes the convergence toward internal belief states by inducing representational contractivity via gradient coupling. However, we reveal that standard MTP often suffers from structural hallucinations, where discrete token supervision encourages illegal shortcuts in latent space that violate environmental constraints. To address this, we propose a novel method Latent Semantic Enhancement MTP (LSE-MTP), which anchors predictions to ground-truth hidden state trajectories. Experiments on synthetic graphs and real-world Manhattan Taxi Ride show that LSE-MTP effectively bridges the gap between discrete tokens and continuous state representations, enhancing representation alignment, reducing structural hallucinations, and improving robustness to perturbations.

</details>


### [106] [Target Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06159)
*Jean Kaddour*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出目标策略优化（TPO），一种通过分离"哪些补全应获得概率质量"与"参数如何更新"两个问题来解决强化学习优化不稳定性的新算法。TPO基于旧策略和得分构建目标分布q_i ∝ p_i^old * exp(u_i)，并通过交叉熵损失拟合该目标。实验表明TPO在稀疏奖励场景下显著优于PG、PPO、GRPO和DG等基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准策略梯度方法同时处理补全选择概率分配和参数更新，导致优化过程对学习率、梯度裁剪等超参数敏感，容易出现overshoot或undershoot现象，影响算法稳定性和收敛性，尤其在稀疏奖励环境中表现受限。

Method: TPO采用两阶段解耦策略：1）目标构建阶段：基于旧策略p^old和完成项得分u_i构造目标分布q_i ∝ p_i^old * exp(u_i)；2）策略拟合阶段：通过最小化交叉熵损失使当前策略逼近目标分布。其梯度形式为p^θ - q，当策略完全匹配目标时梯度自然消失，确保了训练稳定性。

Result: 在表格老虎机、Transformer序列任务和十亿参数大语言模型RLVR任务上的实验显示：TPO在简单任务上与PG、PPO、GRPO和DG性能相当；在稀疏奖励条件下，TPO显著优于所有基线方法。

Conclusion: TPO通过解耦概率质量分配与参数更新机制，实现了更稳定高效的强化学习优化，特别适用于稀疏奖励场景，为大语言模型的后训练提供了有效的新范式。

Abstract: In RL, given a prompt, we sample a group of completions from a model and score them. Two questions follow: which completions should gain probability mass, and how should the parameters move to realize that change? Standard policy-gradient methods answer both at once, so the update can overshoot or undershoot depending on the learning rate, clipping, and other optimizer choices. We introduce \emph{Target Policy Optimization} (TPO), which separates the two questions. Given scored completions, TPO constructs a target distribution $q_i \propto p_i^{\,\mathrm{old}} \exp(u_i)$ and fits the policy to it by cross-entropy. The loss gradient on sampled-completion logits is $p^θ- q$, which vanishes once the policy matches the target. On tabular bandits, transformer sequence tasks, and billion-parameter LLM RLVR, TPO matches PG, PPO, GRPO, and DG on easy tasks and substantially outperforms them under sparse reward. Code is available at https://github.com/JeanKaddour/tpo.

</details>


### [107] [Topological Characterization of Churn Flow and Unsupervised Correction to the Wu Flow-Regime Map in Small-Diameter Vertical Pipes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06167)
*Brady Koenig,Sushovan Majhi,Atish Mitra,Abigail Stein,Burt Todd*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究首次利用欧拉特征曲面(ECS)和多重核学习(MKL)为垂直两相流中的搅拌流提供了定量数学定义。通过融合拓扑特征与气相速度，在无监督条件下实现了95.6%的四分类准确率和100%的搅拌流召回率，性能媲美需要数千标注样本的监督方法，并揭示了现有机理模型在小直径管道中段塞流持续性预测不足的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 搅拌流作为垂直两相流中的混沌振荡流态，40多年来始终缺乏定量数学定义。现有机理模型在直径较小的管道中普遍低估段塞流的持续性，其根本原因在于界面张力和管壁相互作用占主导地位，而传统特征难以捕捉此类复杂拓扑结构变化。亟需一种能够客观表征流型拓扑本质的新方法。

Method: 将无监督流型发现建模为多重核学习(MKL)框架，融合两类ECS衍生核函数：基于χ(s,t)曲面的L¹距离时间对齐核，以及尺度相关的振幅统计核(均值、标准差、最大值、最小值)，并与气相速度特征加权组合。在蒙大拿理工37组未标记空气-水实验数据上进行自校准权重学习，并在德州农工大学947张图像和45组伪实验上完成跨设施验证。

Result: 学习得到最优权重β_ECS=0.14、β_amp=0.50、β_ugs=0.36，其中拓扑衍生特征总权重占比达64%；ECS推断的段塞/搅拌转变点比Wu等(2017)预测值高3.81 m/s，定量证实了现有模型在小管径中的预测偏差；跨设施验证显示搅拌流拓扑复杂度是段塞流的1.9倍(p < 10⁻⁵)；在45组伪实验中实现95.6%四分类准确率和100%搅拌流召回率，性能超越依赖数千标注样本的监督基准。

Conclusion: 本研究首次建立了搅拌流的数学定义，证明了无监督拓扑描述符能够有效挑战并修正广泛采用的机理模型。结果表明，基于欧拉特征曲面的拓扑表征不仅为流型识别提供了新范式，更揭示了现有物理模型在复杂界面动力学方面的认知局限，为两相流研究开辟了数据驱动与物理知识融合的新路径。

Abstract: Churn flow-the chaotic, oscillatory regime in vertical two-phase flow-has lacked a quantitative mathematical definition for over $40$ years. We introduce the first topology-based characterization using Euler Characteristic Surfaces (ECS). We formulate unsupervised regime discovery as Multiple Kernel Learning (MKL), blending two complementary ECS-derived kernels-temporal alignment ($L^1$ distance on the $χ(s,t)$ surface) and amplitude statistics (scale-wise mean, standard deviation, max, min)-with gas velocity. Applied to $37$ unlabeled air-water trials from Montana Tech, the self-calibrating framework learns weights $β_{ECS}=0.14$, $β_{amp}=0.50$, $β_{ugs}=0.36$, placing $64\%$ of total weight on topology-derived features ($β_{ECS} + β_{amp}$). The ECS-inferred slug/churn transition lies $+3.81$ m/s above Wu et al.'s (2017) prediction in $2$-in. tubing, quantifying reports that existing models under-predict slug persistence in small-diameter pipes where interfacial tension and wall-to-wall interactions dominate flow. Cross-facility validation on $947$ Texas A&M University images confirms $1.9\times$ higher topological complexity in churn vs. slug ($p < 10^{-5}$). Applied to $45$ TAMU pseudo-trials, the same unsupervised framework achieves $95.6\%$ $4$-class accuracy and $100\%$ churn recall-without any labeled training data-matching or exceeding supervised baselines that require thousands of annotated examples. This work provides the first mathematical definition of churn flow and demonstrates that unsupervised topological descriptors can challenge and correct widely adopted mechanistic models.

</details>


### [108] [In-Place Test-Time Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06169)
*Guhao Feng,Shengjie Luo,Kai Hua,Ge Zhang,Di He,Wenhao Huang,Tianle Cai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出原地测试时训练(In-Place TTT)框架，通过将MLP块的最终投影矩阵作为快速权重，实现LLM推理时的参数动态更新。该方法采用与下一词预测任务对齐的自定义目标函数和高效分块更新机制，使4B参数模型在128k上下文任务上性能显著提升，为LLM持续学习提供了新范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统"训练后部署"范式限制了LLM对实时信息流进行动态适应的能力。现有测试时训练(TTT)方法虽能更新推理时的快速权重，但面临架构不兼容、计算效率低下以及目标函数与语言建模任务不匹配等关键障碍，阻碍了其在当前LLM生态系统中的实际应用。

Method: 1) 将MLP块的最终投影矩阵作为可适应的快速权重，实现无需重训练的"即插即用"增强；2) 用理论支撑、与自回归语言建模的下一词预测任务明确对齐的目标函数替代TTT的通用重建目标；3) 采用高效的分块更新机制，实现与上下文并行兼容的高可扩展算法。

Result: 1) 作为原地增强，4B参数模型在长达128k上下文的任务上实现卓越性能；2) 从头预训练时持续优于现有竞争TTT方法；3) 消融研究验证了各项设计选择的合理性。

Conclusion: In-Place TTT通过无缝赋予LLM测试时训练能力，解决了静态部署范式的根本局限，同时保持了计算效率和架构兼容性，为构建持续学习的LLM新范式提供了有希望的前进方向。

Abstract: The static ``train then deploy" paradigm fundamentally limits Large Language Models (LLMs) from dynamically adapting their weights in response to continuous streams of new information inherent in real-world tasks. Test-Time Training (TTT) offers a compelling alternative by updating a subset of model parameters (fast weights) at inference time, yet its potential in the current LLM ecosystem is hindered by critical barriers including architectural incompatibility, computational inefficiency and misaligned fast weight objectives for language modeling. In this work, we introduce In-Place Test-Time Training (In-Place TTT), a framework that seamlessly endows LLMs with Test-Time Training ability. In-Place TTT treats the final projection matrix of the ubiquitous MLP blocks as its adaptable fast weights, enabling a ``drop-in" enhancement for LLMs without costly retraining from scratch. Furthermore, we replace TTT's generic reconstruction objective with a tailored, theoretically-grounded objective explicitly aligned with the Next-Token-Prediction task governing autoregressive language modeling. This principled objective, combined with an efficient chunk-wise update mechanism, results in a highly scalable algorithm compatible with context parallelism. Extensive experiments validate our framework's effectiveness: as an in-place enhancement, it enables a 4B-parameter model to achieve superior performance on tasks with contexts up to 128k, and when pretrained from scratch, it consistently outperforms competitive TTT-related approaches. Ablation study results further provide deeper insights on our design choices. Collectively, our results establish In-Place TTT as a promising step towards a paradigm of continual learning in LLMs.

### [109] [Web Retrieval-Aware Chunking (W-RAC) for Efficient and Cost-Effective Retrieval-Augmented Generation Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04936)
*Uday Allu,Sonu Kedia,Tanmay Odapally,Biddwan Ahmed*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出W-RAC框架，通过将网页解析为结构化ID单元并使用LLM仅做分组决策而非文本生成，实现检索增强生成的成本高效分块，相比传统方法在保持检索性能的同时降低LLM成本达一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统RAG分块方法（固定大小、基于规则或全智能体）在处理大规模网页内容时存在高token消耗、冗余文本生成、可扩展性有限和可调试性差等问题，亟需一种更高效的解决方案。

Method: W-RAC框架将文本提取与语义分块规划解耦，将解析后的网页内容表示为结构化、ID可寻址单元，利用大语言模型仅进行检索感知的分组决策而非文本生成。

Result: 实验分析表明，W-RAC在实现与基线方法相当或更优检索性能的同时，将分块相关的LLM成本降低了一个数量级。

Conclusion: W-RAC是一种专为网页文档设计的新型成本高效分块框架，通过架构创新显著降低了token使用和幻觉风险，同时提高了系统可观测性，为大规模RAG系统提供了更优的解决方案。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) systems critically depend on effective document chunking strategies to balance retrieval quality, latency, and operational cost. Traditional chunking approaches, such as fixed-size, rule-based, or fully agentic chunking, often suffer from high token consumption, redundant text generation, limited scalability, and poor debuggability, especially for large-scale web content ingestion. In this paper, we propose Web Retrieval-Aware Chunking (W-RAC), a novel, cost-efficient chunking framework designed specifically for web-based documents. W-RAC decouples text extraction from semantic chunk planning by representing parsed web content as structured, ID-addressable units and leveraging large language models (LLMs) only for retrieval-aware grouping decisions rather than text generation. This significantly reduces token usage, eliminates hallucination risks, and improves system observability.Experimental analysis and architectural comparison demonstrate that W-RAC achieves comparable or better retrieval performance than traditional chunking approaches while reducing chunking-related LLM costs by an order of magnitude.

### [110] [SUMMIR: A Hallucination-Aware Framework for Ranking Sports Insights from LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04947)
*Nitish Kumar,Sannu Kumar,S Akash,Manish Gupta,Ankith Karat,Sriparna Saha*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对在线体育新闻快速扩张，本文构建自动化洞察提取框架。收集4大体育项目7900篇报道，利用多款先进大模型生成赛前赛后洞察，通过FactScore和SummaC双重验证确保事实性，提出SUMMIR模型实现基于用户兴趣的智能排序，为体育新闻处理提供可靠解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着在线体育新闻迅速普及，从赛前赛后报道中自动提取有价值的洞察对于提升用户参与度和理解能力至关重要。传统人工提取效率低下且难以规模化，亟需自动化解决方案来处理海量体育新闻内容，实现个性化信息服务的精准触达。

Method: 采用多阶段方法：1)构建包含板球、足球、篮球、棒球4大项目800场比赛的7900篇文章数据集；2)设计两步验证流程结合开源与闭源大模型确保上下文相关性；3)使用GPT-4o、Qwen2.5-72B-Instruct、Llama-3.3-70B-Instruct和Mixtral-8x7B-Instruct-v0.1生成综合洞察；4)采用FactScore评估事实准确性，SummaC框架结合GPT-4o进行幻觉检测；5)提出SUMMIR（句子统一多度量重要性排序模型）架构，根据用户特定兴趣对洞察进行排序。

Result: 实验表明该框架能有效生成高质量、相关性强的洞察。关键发现：不同大模型在事实一致性和趣味性上存在显著差异，GPT-4o等闭源模型表现优于开源模型；SUMMIR能根据用户偏好实现个性化排序；双重验证机制有效降低了幻觉率，FactScore与SummaC的结合提供了更全面的质量评估。

Conclusion: 本研究贡献了体育新闻自动化洞察生成的稳健框架，验证了多模型协同与双重验证机制的有效性。研究揭示了当前大模型在体育领域的事实性表现差异，为模型选择和应用提供重要参考。开源代码将促进后续研究，推动体育新闻智能化处理技术的发展与应用。

Abstract: With the rapid proliferation of online sports journalism, extracting meaningful pre-game and post-game insights from articles is essential for enhancing user engagement and comprehension. In this paper, we address the task of automatically extracting such insights from articles published before and after matches. We curate a dataset of 7,900 news articles covering 800 matches across four major sports: Cricket, Soccer, Basketball, and Baseball. To ensure contextual relevance, we employ a two-step validation pipeline leveraging both open-source and proprietary large language models (LLMs). We then utilize multiple state-of-the-art LLMs (GPT-4o, Qwen2.5-72B-Instruct, Llama-3.3-70B-Instruct, and Mixtral-8x7B-Instruct-v0.1) to generate comprehensive insights. The factual accuracy of these outputs is rigorously assessed using a FactScore-based methodology, complemented by hallucination detection via the SummaC (Summary Consistency) framework with GPT-4o. Finally, we propose SUMMIR (Sentence Unified Multimetric Model for Importance Ranking), a novel architecture designed to rank insights based on user-specific interests. Our results demonstrate the effectiveness of this approach in generating high-quality, relevant insights, while also revealing significant differences in factual consistency and interestingness across LLMs. This work contributes a robust framework for automated, reliable insight generation from sports news content. The source code is availble here https://github.com/nitish-iitp/SUMMIR.

### [111] [From PDF to RAG-Ready: Evaluating Document Conversion Frameworks for Domain-Specific Question Answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04948)
*José Guilherme Marques dos Santos,Ricardo Yang,Rui Humberto Pereira,Alexandre Sousa,Brígida Mónica Faria,Henrique Lopes Cardoso,José Duarte,José Luís Reis,Luís Paulo Reis,Pedro Pimenta,José Paulo Marques dos Santos*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本研究系统评估了四种开源PDF转Markdown框架在RAG问答系统中的表现，发现数据预处理质量是性能关键决定因素。Docling配合层次化分块和图像描述达到94.1%的准确率，接近人工标注的97.1%。元数据丰富化与层次感知分块比单纯选择转换框架贡献更大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究对比了Docling、MinerU、Marker和DeepSeek OCR四种开源PDF转Markdown框架，测试了19种不同配置（包括转换工具、清洗变换、分块策略和元数据丰富化）。评估使用36份葡萄牙行政文档（1706页，约49.2万词）构成的基准测试集，包含50个问题，采用LLM-as-judge评分方式并取10次运行平均值。

Result: Docling配合层次化分块和图像描述获得最高自动化准确率94.1%，仅低于人工Markdown的97.1%。元数据丰富化和层次感知分块对准确率的贡献超过转换框架选择本身。基于字体的层次重建方法一致优于基于LLM的方法。探索性GraphRAG实现得分仅82%，表现逊于基础RAG。

Conclusion: 数据准备质量是RAG系统性能的支配性因素。研究强调了在PDF预处理中采用层次化分块、元数据丰富化和字体感知结构重建的重要性，同时表明当前朴素知识图谱构建方法尚不成熟，其复杂性尚未能带来相应性能提升。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) systems depend critically on the quality of document preprocessing, yet no prior study has evaluated PDF processing frameworks by their impact on downstream question-answering accuracy. We address this gap through a systematic comparison of four open-source PDF-to-Markdown conversion frameworks, Docling, MinerU, Marker, and DeepSeek OCR, across 19 pipeline configurations for extracting text and other contents from PDFs, varying the conversion tool, cleaning transformations, splitting strategy, and metadata enrichment. Evaluation was performed using a manually curated 50-question benchmark over a corpus of 36 Portuguese administrative documents (1,706 pages, ~492K words), with LLM-as-judge scoring averaged over 10 runs. Two baselines bounded the results: naïve PDFLoader (86.9%) and manually curated Markdown (97.1%). Docling with hierarchical splitting and image descriptions achieved the highest automated accuracy (94.1%). Metadata enrichment and hierarchy-aware chunking contributed more to accuracy than the conversion framework choice alone. Font-based hierarchy rebuilding consistently outperformed LLM-based approaches. An exploratory GraphRAG implementation scored only 82%, underperforming basic RAG, suggesting that naïve knowledge graph construction without ontological guidance does not yet justify its added complexity. These findings demonstrate that data preparation quality is the dominant factor in RAG system performance.

### [112] [MG$^2$-RAG: Multi-Granularity Graph for Multimodal Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04969)
*Sijun Dai,Qiang Huang,Xiaoxing You,Jun Yu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: MG²-RAG是一个轻量级多粒度图检索增强生成框架，通过构建分层多模态知识图谱和引入多粒度图检索机制，解决了现有系统在复杂跨模态推理中的局限性，在四个多模态任务上实现SOTA性能，同时图构建速度提升43.3倍，成本降低23.9倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG系统在处理多模态大语言模型时面临两大挑战：扁平向量检索忽略结构依赖关系，而基于图的方法依赖昂贵的"翻译为文本"流程且丢失细粒度视觉信息。因此需要一种能保留视觉细节、支持结构化推理且高效的多模态RAG框架。

Method: 提出MG²-RAG框架，主要包括两个创新：(1) 通过轻量级文本解析与实体驱动视觉定位构建分层多模态知识图谱，将文本实体与视觉区域融合为统一的多模态节点，保留原子证据；(2) 设计多粒度图检索机制，聚合密集相似度并在图上传播相关性，支持结构化多跳推理。

Result: 在检索、知识型VQA、推理和分类四项多模态任务上均达到SOTA性能；图构建开销显著降低，相比先进图基框架平均加速43.3倍，成本降低23.9倍。

Conclusion: MG²-RAG通过统一的多模态图表示和高效检索机制，有效提升了MLLMs的跨模态推理能力，同时大幅降低了计算成本，为多模态RAG系统提供了可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) mitigates hallucinations in Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs), yet existing systems struggle with complex cross-modal reasoning. Flat vector retrieval often ignores structural dependencies, while current graph-based methods rely on costly ``translation-to-text'' pipelines that discard fine-grained visual information. To address these limitations, we propose \textbf{MG$^2$-RAG}, a lightweight \textbf{M}ulti-\textbf{G}ranularity \textbf{G}raph \textbf{RAG} framework that jointly improves graph construction, modality fusion, and cross-modal retrieval. MG$^2$-RAG constructs a hierarchical multimodal knowledge graph by combining lightweight textual parsing with entity-driven visual grounding, enabling textual entities and visual regions to be fused into unified multimodal nodes that preserve atomic evidence. Building on this representation, we introduce a multi-granularity graph retrieval mechanism that aggregates dense similarities and propagates relevance across the graph to support structured multi-hop reasoning. Extensive experiments across four representative multimodal tasks (i.e., retrieval, knowledge-based VQA, reasoning, and classification) demonstrate that MG$^2$-RAG consistently achieves state-of-the-art performance while reducing graph construction overhead with an average 43.3$\times$ speedup and 23.9$\times$ cost reduction compared with advanced graph-based frameworks.

### [114] [CURE:Circuit-Aware Unlearning for LLM-based Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04982)
*Ziheng Chen,Jiali Cheng,Zezhong Fan,Hadi Amiri,Yunzhi Yao,Xiangguo Sun,Yang Zhang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对大语言模型推荐系统面临的隐私风险，本文提出CURE框架，通过识别任务因果计算子图（circuit），将模型参数解耦为遗忘专用、保留专用和任务共享三组，并施以差异化的更新规则，以缓解梯度冲突，实现更有效的机器遗忘。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着隐私法规收紧，大语言模型推荐系统（LLMRec）中用户数据的引入带来重大隐私风险，机器遗忘算法成为实际部署的关键。然而现有方法将遗忘与保留目标加权组合并统一更新参数，导致梯度冲突、优化不稳定，造成遗忘无效或模型效用严重退化，且过程不透明，缺乏可信度。

Method: 提出电路感知的遗忘框架CURE：首先提取物品推荐的核心因果计算子图（circuit），分析其中各模块对遗忘与保留目标的贡献；进而将模块划分为遗忘专用、保留专用和任务共享三类；对每类模块设计功能特定的更新规则，以分离优化目标，减轻梯度冲突。

Result: 在真实数据集上的实验表明，与现有基线方法相比，CURE能够实现更有效的机器遗忘，同时隐式地更好地保持了模型效用。

Conclusion: CURE通过电路感知的参数解耦与选择性更新，为LLMRec提供了一种高效、透明的遗忘方案，解决了梯度冲突与效用退化的关键问题，为隐私保护的大模型推荐部署提供了新思路。

Abstract: Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) have opened new opportunities for recommender systems by enabling rich semantic understanding and reasoning about user interests and item attributes. However, as privacy regulations tighten, incorporating user data into LLM-based recommendation (LLMRec) introduces significant privacy risks, making unlearning algorithms increasingly crucial for practical deployment. Despite growing interest in LLMRec unlearning, most existing approaches formulate unlearning as a weighted combination of forgetting and retaining objectives while updating model parameters in a uniform manner. Such formulations inevitably induce gradient conflicts between the two objectives, leading to unstable optimization and resulting in either ineffective unlearning or severe degradation of model utility. Moreover, the unlearning procedure remains largely black-box, undermining its transparency and trustworthiness. To tackle these challenges, we propose CURE, a circuit-aware unlearning framework that disentangles model components into functionally distinct subsets and selectively updates them. Here, a circuit refers to a computational subgraph that is causally responsible for task-specific behaviors. Specifically, we extract the core circuits underlying item recommendation and analyze how individual modules within these circuits contribute to the forget and retain objectives. Based on this analysis, these modules are categorized into forget-specific, retain-specific, and task-shared groups, each subject to function-specific update rules to mitigate gradient conflicts during unlearning. Experiments on real-world datasets show that our approach achieves more effective unlearning than existing baselines.

*Zezhong Fan,Ziheng Chen,Luyi Ma,Jin Huang,Lalitesh Morishetti,Kaushiki Nag,Sushant Kumar,Kannan Achan*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式推荐虽在多任务中性能优异，但存在严重且会加剧的流行度偏差，损害推荐公平性与多样性，亟需深入探究成因并设计去偏方案。

Method: 提出CRAB后处理策略：先分割过流行token重构码本并保留层次语义结构；再引入树结构正则化器增强语义一致性，促进不流行token学习更丰富表示。

Result: 在真实数据集上的实验表明，CRAB显著提升推荐性能，有效缓解流行度偏差，验证了方法的有效性。

Abstract: Generative recommendation (GeneRec) has introduced a new paradigm that represents items as discrete semantic tokens and predicts items in a generative manner. Despite its strong performance across multiple recommendation tasks, existing GeneRec approaches still suffer from severe popularity bias and may even exacerbate it. In this work, we conduct a comprehensive empirical analysis to uncover the root causes of this phenomenon, yielding two core insights: 1) imbalanced tokenization inherits and can further amplify popularity bias from historical item interactions; 2) current training procedures disproportionately favor popular tokens while neglecting semantic relationships among tokens, thereby intensifying popularity bias. Building on these insights, we propose CRAB, a post-hoc debiasing strategy for GeneRec that alleviates popularity bias by mitigating frequency imbalance among semantic tokens. Specifically, given a well-trained model, we first rebalance the codebook by splitting over-popular tokens while preserving their hierarchical semantic structure. Based on the adjusted codebook, we further introduce a tree-structured regularizer to enhance semantic consistency, encouraging more informative representations for unpopular tokens during training. Experiments on real-world datasets demonstrate that CRAB significantly improves recommendation performance by effectively alleviating popularity bias.

### [116] [Offline RL for Adaptive Policy Retrieval in Prior Authorization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05125)
*Ruslan Sharifullin,Maxim Gorshkov,Hannah Clay*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 将医保预授权政策检索建模为MDP问题，通过离线RL训练自适应检索策略。CQL、IQL和DPO三种方法均显著优于静态top-K基线，其中DPO在保持92%准确率的同时减少47%检索步骤，达到帕累托前沿的最优平衡。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将政策检索建模为马尔可夫决策过程(MDP)，智能体迭代选择top-K候选块或停止决策。采用保守Q学习(CQL)、隐式Q学习(IQL)和直接偏好优化(DPO)三种离线强化学习方法，在基于CMS公开数据生成的合成PA请求轨迹上进行训练，奖励函数平衡决策正确性与检索成本。

Conclusion: 自适应检索策略显著优于静态基线，其中DPO在准确率-效率权衡中表现最佳，能在保持高准确率的同时大幅减少检索步骤，为医保预授权政策检索提供了更优的解决方案。

Abstract: Prior authorization (PA) requires interpretation of complex and fragmented coverage policies, yet existing retrieval-augmented systems rely on static top-$K$ strategies with fixed numbers of retrieved sections. Such fixed retrieval can be inefficient and gather irrelevant or insufficient information. We model policy retrieval for PA as a sequential decision-making problem, formulating adaptive retrieval as a Markov Decision Process (MDP). In our system, an agent iteratively selects policy chunks from a top-$K$ candidate set or chooses to stop and issue a decision. The reward balances decision correctness against retrieval cost, capturing the trade-off between accuracy and efficiency. We train policies using Conservative Q-Learning (CQL), Implicit Q-Learning (IQL), and Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) in an offline RL setting on logged trajectories generated from baseline retrieval strategies over synthetic PA requests derived from publicly available CMS coverage data. On a corpus of 186 policy chunks spanning 10 CMS procedures, CQL achieves 92% decision accuracy (+30 percentage points over the best fixed-$K$ baseline) via exhaustive retrieval, while IQL matches the best baseline accuracy using 44% fewer retrieval steps and achieves the only positive episodic return among all policies. Transition-level DPO matches CQL's 92% accuracy while using 47% fewer retrieval steps (10.6 vs. 20.0), occupying a "selective-accurate" region on the Pareto frontier that dominates both CQL and BC. A behavioral cloning baseline matches CQL, confirming that advantage-weighted or preference-based policy extraction is needed to learn selective retrieval. Lambda ablation over step costs $λ\in \{0.05, 0.1, 0.2\}$ reveals a clear accuracy-efficiency inflection: only at $λ= 0.2$ does CQL transition from exhaustive to selective retrieval.

### [117] [Entities as Retrieval Signals: A Systematic Study of Coverage, Supervision, and Evaluation in Entity-Oriented Ranking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05204)
*Shubham Chatterjee*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 研究发现实体导向检索评估结果不一致的根源在于评估方法本身，而非模型失效。在TREC Robust04上测试的443个系统中，开放世界评估下MAP提升均不超过0.05，实体通道的覆盖率与区分度不可兼得是核心瓶颈。关键理论贡献在于区分了概念实体相关性(CER)与可观测实体相关性(OER)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究实体导向检索评估结果相互矛盾的深层原因，明确这种不一致性究竟源于模型架构的局限性还是评估范式的缺陷。

Method: 在TREC Robust04数据集上，系统评估了6种神经重排序器与437种无监督配置相对于BM25的性能差异，通过对比条件性（实体受限）与开放世界（完整候选集）两种评估设置进行深入分析。

Result: 443个系统在开放世界评估下MAP提升均≤0.05；最佳配置性能与官方最优系统持平且超越多数神经重排序器；实体信号存在根本性瓶颈，理想选择下仅覆盖19.7%相关文档，无方法能同时实现高覆盖率与高区分度；所有监督策略仅作用于概念实体相关性(CER)层面，忽略链接环境，导致信号语义有效但判别性不足。

Conclusion: 条件性与开放世界评估回答的是不同科学问题，当前研究常将二者混淆。领域进展需要具备实体级区分度的数据集及同时报告覆盖率与效果的评估方式。条件性增益不能外推至开放世界有效性，而开放世界失败亦不能否定实体模型本身价值。

Abstract: Entity-oriented retrieval assumes that relevant documents exhibit query-relevant entities, yet evaluations report conflicting results. We show this inconsistency stems not from model failure, but from evaluation.
  On TREC Robust04, we evaluate six neural rerankers and 437 unsupervised configurations against BM25. Across 443 systems, none improves MAP by more than 0.05 under open-world evaluation over the full candidate set, despite strong gains under entity-restricted settings. The best configuration matches the official Robust04 best system and outperforms most neural rerankers, indicating that the architecture is not the limiting factor. Instead, the bottleneck is the entity channel: even under idealized selection, entity signals cover only 19.7\% of relevant documents, and no method achieves both high coverage and discrimination.
  We explain this via a distinction between Conceptual Entity Relevance (CER) -- semantic relatedness -- and Observable Entity Relevance (OER) -- corpus-grounded discriminativeness under a given linker. All supervision strategies operate at the CER level and ignore the linking environment, leading to signals that are semantically valid but not discriminative. Improving supervision therefore does not recover open-world performance: stronger signals reduce coverage without improving effectiveness.
  Conditional and open-world evaluation answer different questions: exploiting entity evidence versus improving retrieval under realistic linking, but are often conflated. Progress requires datasets with entity-level discriminativeness and evaluation that reports both coverage and effectiveness. Until then, conditional gains do not imply open-world effectiveness, and open-world failures do not invalidate entity-based models.

### [118] [Spike Hijacking in Late-Interaction Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05253)
*Karthik Suresh,Tushar Vatsa,Tracy King,Asim Kadav,Michael Friedrich*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该研究通过机制分析揭示MaxSim池化导致梯度过度集中，存在稀疏性与鲁棒性的权衡，促使硬最大池化在后期交互检索中被更优替代。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究后期交互检索中硬最大相似度(MaxSim)池化对训练动态的结构性偏置，及其对模型鲁棒性的潜在负面影响。

Method: 采用受控合成环境下的批次内对比训练，对比MaxSim与Top-k、softmax等平滑聚合方式的梯度路由特性，并在真实多向量检索基准上通过文档长度扫描验证。

Result: 实验证明MaxSim诱导显著的patch级梯度集中，虽提升早期判别力但加剧长度敏感性，性能随文档增长衰减更显著；真实基准验证了硬最大池化的脆弱性。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了MaxSim梯度集中是后期交互检索的结构性属性，确立了稀疏性与鲁棒性的根本权衡，为设计原则性替代方案提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Late-interaction retrieval models rely on hard maximum similarity (MaxSim) to aggregate token-level similarities. Although effective, this winner-take-all pooling rule may structurally bias training dynamics. We provide a mechanistic study of gradient routing and robustness in MaxSim-based retrieval. In a controlled synthetic environment with in-batch contrastive training, we demonstrate that MaxSim induces significantly higher patch-level gradient concentration than smoother alternatives such as Top-k pooling and softmax aggregation. While sparse routing can improve early discrimination, it also increases sensitivity to document length: as the number of document patches grows, MaxSim degrades more sharply than mild smoothing variants. We corroborate these findings on a real-world multi-vector retrieval benchmark, where controlled document-length sweeps reveal similar brittleness under hard max pooling. Together, our results isolate pooling-induced gradient concentration as a structural property of late-interaction retrieval and highlight a sparsity-robustness tradeoff. These findings motivate principled alternatives to hard max pooling in multi-vector retrieval systems.

### [119] [Pay Attention to Sequence Split: Uncovering the Impacts of Sub-Sequence Splitting on Sequential Recommendation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05309)
*Yizhou Dang,Yifan Wu,Minhan Huang,Chuang Zhao,Lianbo Ma,Guibing Guo,Xingwei Wang,Zhu Sun*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本研究发现子序列分割(SSS)会干扰序列推荐模型的评估真实性，其效果高度依赖于分割方法、目标策略与损失函数的特定组合。实验表明移除SSS后SOTA模型性能显著下降甚至低于传统模型。研究揭示了SSS通过均衡数据分布和提升物品曝光多样性来提升性能，并呼吁建立更公平的评估标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究虽证实子序列分割可缓解序列推荐的数据稀疏性，但作者发现许多SOTA模型在数据读取阶段隐式使用SSS（论文未提及），这严重影响了性能评估的公平性。此现象引发了对SSS真实有效性、适用边界及作用机制的深入探究需求。

Method: 采用控制变量实验设计，系统性地移除和添加SSS操作，对比分析不同模型架构下的性能变化；通过枚举分割方法、目标策略和损失函数的不同组合，识别有效配置模式；从训练数据分布统计角度定量解释SSS的性能增益机制。

Result: 发现SSS存在评估干扰效应：当禁用SSS时，多个SOTA模型性能显著下降，甚至不及早期经典模型；识别出SSS的"组合有效性"：仅在特定的分割方法、目标策略与损失函数协同使用时才有效，错误组合会损害性能；揭示SSS的作用机理：通过平衡训练数据分布并增加不同物品作为预测目标的概率，从而缓解数据稀疏性。

Conclusion: 研究质疑了当前序列推荐领域的评估规范，建议采用更透明和统一的数据处理流程，并提供SSS干扰缓解方案。同时探讨了数据增强方法，为未来更严谨的模型评估体系建立提供理论基础和实践指导。

Abstract: Sub-sequence splitting (SSS) has been demonstrated as an effective approach to mitigate data sparsity in sequential recommendation (SR) by splitting a raw user interaction sequence into multiple sub-sequences. Previous studies have demonstrated its ability to enhance the performance of SR models significantly. However, in this work, we discover that \textbf{(i). SSS may interfere with the evaluation of the model's actual performance.} We observed that many recent state-of-the-art SR models employ SSS during the data reading stage (not mentioned in the papers). When we removed this operation, performance significantly declined, even falling below that of earlier classical SR models. The varying improvements achieved by SSS and different splitting methods across different models prompt us to analyze further when SSS proves effective. We find that \textbf{(ii). SSS demonstrates strong capabilities only when specific splitting methods, target strategies, and loss functions are used together.} Inappropriate combinations may even harm performance. Furthermore, we analyze why sub-sequence splitting yields such remarkable performance gains and find that \textbf{(iii). it evens out the distribution of training data while increasing the likelihood that different items are targeted.} Finally, we provide suggestions for overcoming SSS interference, along with a discussion on data augmentation methods and future directions. We hope this work will prompt the broader community to re-examine the impact of data splitting on SR and promote fairer, more rigorous model evaluation. All analysis code and data will be made available upon acceptance. We provide a simple, anonymous implementation at https://github.com/KingGugu/SSS4SR.

</details>


### [120] [Next-Scale Generative Reranking: A Tree-based Generative Rerank Method at Meituan](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05314)
*Shuli Wang,Changhao Li,Ke Fan,Senjie Kou Junwei Yin,Chi Wang,Yinhua Zhu,Haitao Wang,Xingxing Wang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该论文提出现代多阶段推荐系统中的重排序问题，指出生成式范式存在两大缺陷：生成器缺乏局部与全局视角，以及训练时生成器与评估器目标不一致。为此提出基于树的NSGR框架，通过"下一尺度生成器"实现由粗到精的列表扩展，并设计多尺度评估器提供尺度特定的监督信号。在公开和工业数据集上的实验验证其有效性，并已部署于美团外卖平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代推荐系统重排序建模中，生成式方法虽能处理组合空间复杂度问题，但仍面临两个核心挑战：一是无论自回归还是非自回归策略，生成器均因缺乏局部与全局视角而无法产生最优排序结果；二是训练阶段生成器与评估器之间存在目标不一致问题，导致监督信号复杂化，影响模型性能。

Method: 提出NSGR（Next-Scale Generation Reranking）树状生成框架：1）设计"下一尺度生成器"（NSG），从用户兴趣出发以由粗到精方式逐步扩展推荐列表，平衡全局与局部视角；2）构建基于树的多尺度评估器（MSE），设计多尺度邻域损失函数，为NSG在每个尺度上提供尺度特定的监督指导。

Result: 在公开数据集和工业数据集上的大量实验验证了NSGR的有效性；该模型已成功部署于美团外卖平台，展现了实际工业应用价值。

Conclusion: NSGR通过树状结构和多尺度协同训练机制，有效解决了生成式重排序中视角局限与目标不一致两大问题，为推荐系统重排序提供了新的框架思路，并具备显著的工业落地潜力。

Abstract: In modern multi-stage recommendation systems, reranking plays a critical role by modeling contextual information. Due to inherent challenges such as the combinatorial space complexity, an increasing number of methods adopt the generative paradigm: the generator produces the optimal list during inference, while an evaluator guides the generator's optimization during the training phase. However, these methods still face two problems. Firstly, these generators fail to produce optimal generation results due to the lack of both local and global perspectives, regardless of whether the generation strategy is autoregressive or non-autoregressive. Secondly, the goal inconsistency problem between the generator and the evaluator during training complicates the guidance signal and leading to suboptimal performance. To address these issues, we propose the \textbf{N}ext-\textbf{S}cale \textbf{G}eneration \textbf{R}eranking (NSGR), a tree-based generative framework. Specifically, we introduce a next-scale generator (NSG) that progressively expands a recommendation list from user interests in a coarse-to-fine manner, balancing global and local perspectives. Furthermore, we design a multi-scale neighbor loss, which leverages a tree-based multi-scale evaluator (MSE) to provide scale-specific guidance to the NSG at each scale. Extensive experiments on public and industrial datasets validate the effectiveness of NSGR. And NSGR has been successfully deployed on the Meituan food delivery platform.

### [121] [Semantic Trimming and Auxiliary Multi-step Prediction for Generative Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05329)
*Tianyu Zhan,Kairui Fu,Chengfei Lv,Zheqi Lv,Shengyu Zhang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对基于语义ID(SID)的生成式推荐系统在高粒度编码下出现的训练开销巨大与性能不稳定问题，本文提出STAMP框架。该框架通过输入端的语义自适应剪枝(SAP)去除冗余令牌，以及输出端的多步辅助预测(MAP)增强监督信号密度，有效缓解"语义稀释效应"，在显著降低计算成本的同时保持或提升推荐性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式推荐已从原子索引转向语义ID(SID)框架以增强泛化能力，但高粒度SIDs导致序列扩展引发训练开销剧增，并伴随非单调精度波动的性能不稳定现象。作者揭示这些问题的根本原因在于"语义稀释效应"——冗余令牌消耗大量计算并稀释稀疏的学习信号，因此需同时提升输入信息密度与输出监督信号密度。

Method: 提出STAMP（语义修剪与多步辅助预测）框架，采用双端优化策略：输入端采用语义自适应剪枝(SAP)，在前向传播中动态过滤冗余令牌，将噪声序列转化为紧凑的高信息密度表示；输出端采用多步辅助预测(MAP)，通过多令牌联合预测目标密集化反馈信号，增强长程依赖建模能力。通过统一输入净化与信号放大，提升训练效率与表示质量。

Result: 在公开Amazon数据集及大规模工业数据集上的实验表明，STAMP在多种推荐架构下均实现1.23–1.38倍训练加速，VRAM占用降低17.2%–54.7%，同时推荐性能保持不降或有所提升。

Conclusion: STAMP框架通过协同优化输入信息紧凑性与输出监督密集性，有效解决了高粒度语义ID推荐中的语义稀释问题，实现了训练效率与模型性能的双重提升，为生成式推荐系统的工业级应用提供了高效可行的技术方案。

Abstract: Generative Recommendation (GR) has recently transitioned from atomic item-indexing to Semantic ID (SID)-based frameworks to capture intrinsic item relationships and enhance generalization. However, the adoption of high-granularity SIDs leads to two critical challenges: prohibitive training overhead due to sequence expansion and unstable performance reliability characterized by non-monotonic accuracy fluctuations. We identify that these disparate issues are fundamentally rooted in the Semantic Dilution Effect, where redundant tokens waste massive computation and dilute the already sparse learning signals in recommendation. To counteract this, we propose STAMP (Semantic Trimming and Auxiliary Multi-step Prediction), a framework utilizing a dual-end optimization strategy. We argue that effective SID learning requires simultaneously addressing low input information density and sparse output supervision. On the input side, Semantic Adaptive Pruning (SAP) dynamically filters redundancy during the forward pass, converting noise-laden sequences into compact, information-rich representations. On the output side, Multi-step Auxiliary Prediction (MAP) employs a multi-token objective to densify feedback, strengthening long-range dependency capture and ensuring robust learning signals despite compressed inputs. Unifying input purification and signal amplification, STAMP enhances both training efficiency and representation capability. Experiments on public Amazon and large-scale industrial datasets show STAMP achieves 1.23--1.38$\times$ speedup and 17.2\%--54.7\% VRAM reduction while maintaining or improving performance across multiple architectures.

*Xiangchen Pan,Wei Wei*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的可解释推荐方法通常联合预测评分并生成解释，但忽略了这两个目标之间的内在不一致性，导致推荐结果的可信度和透明度不足。为此，需要设计一个能够协调评分预测与解释生成、确保两者一致性的新框架。

Method: 提出Curr-RLCER框架，采用课程学习策略：1) 从基础预测任务（点击率CTR、选择式评分）开始；2) 逐步过渡到开放式推荐解释生成。为每个阶段设计特定的奖励函数以渐进增强推荐系统稳定性，并引入一致性驱动的奖励机制来强制生成解释与预测评分之间的一致性，配合专门设计的评估方案。

Conclusion: 该研究通过课程学习和强化学习相结合的方式，有效解决了可解释推荐中评分预测与解释生成的不一致问题，为构建更透明、可信、可解释的推荐系统提供了新思路。

Abstract: Explainable recommendation systems (RSs) are designed to explicitly uncover the rationale of each recommendation, thereby enhancing the transparency and credibility of RSs. Previous methods often jointly predicted ratings and generated explanations, but overlooked the incoherence of such two objectives. To address this issue, we propose Curr-RLCER, a reinforcement learning framework for explanation coherent recommendation with dynamic rating alignment. It employs curriculum learning, transitioning from basic predictions (i.e., click through rating-CTR, selection-based rating) to open-ended recommendation explanation generation. In particular, the rewards of each stage are designed for progressively enhancing the stability of RSs. Furthermore, a coherence-driven reward mechanism is also proposed to enforce the coherence between generated explanations and predicted ratings, supported by a specifically designed evaluation scheme. The extensive experimental results on three explainable recommendation datasets indicate that the proposed framework is effective. Codes and datasets are available at https://github.com/pxcstart/Curr-RLCER.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Cross-domain Recommendation (CDR) exploits multi-domain correlations to alleviate data sparsity. As a core task within this field, inter-domain recommendation focuses on predicting preferences for users who interact in a source domain but lack behavioral records in a target domain. Existing approaches predominantly rely on overlapping users as anchors for knowledge transfer. In real-world scenarios, overlapping users are often scarce, leaving the vast majority of users with only single-domain interactions. For these users, the absence of explicit alignment signals makes fine-grained preference transfer intrinsically difficult. To address this challenge, this paper proposes Language-Guided Conditional Diffusion for CDR (LGCD), a novel framework that integrates Large Language Models (LLMs) and diffusion models for inter-domain sequential recommendation. Specifically, we leverage LLM reasoning to bridge the domain gap by inferring potential target preferences for single-domain users and mapping them to real items, thereby constructing pseudo-overlapping data. We distinguish between real and pseudo-interaction pathways and introduce additional supervision constraints to mitigate the semantic noise brought by pseudo-interaction. Furthermore, we design a conditional diffusion architecture to precisely guide the generation of target user representations based on source-domain patterns. Extensive experiments demonstrate that LGCD significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods in inter-domain recommendation tasks.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 序列推荐模型在推理阶段面临分布漂移和参数约束导致的实时偏好适应难题，现有测试时训练、增强或微调方法存在计算开销大、增强策略随机或需复杂两阶段训练等局限，亟需实现高效且有效的测试时自适应。

Method: 提出Retrieve-then-Adapt (ReAd)框架：针对测试用户从协同记忆库检索相似物品，通过轻量级检索学习模块生成融合协同信号与预测优化线索的增强嵌入，最终采用融合机制对初始推荐预测进行动态精炼。

Abstract: The sequential recommendation (SR) task aims to predict the next item based on users' historical interaction sequences. Typically trained on historical data, SR models often struggle to adapt to real-time preference shifts during inference due to challenges posed by distributional divergence and parameterized constraints. Existing approaches to address this issue include test-time training, test-time augmentation, and retrieval-augmented fine-tuning. However, these methods either introduce significant computational overhead, rely on random augmentation strategies, or require a carefully designed two-stage training paradigm. In this paper, we argue that the key to effective test-time adaptation lies in achieving both effective augmentation and efficient adaptation. To this end, we propose Retrieve-then-Adapt (ReAd), a novel framework that dynamically adapts a deployed SR model to the test distribution through retrieved user preference signals. Specifically, given a trained SR model, ReAd first retrieves collaboratively similar items for a test user from a constructed collaborative memory database. A lightweight retrieval learning module then integrates these items into an informative augmentation embedding that captures both collaborative signals and prediction-refinement cues. Finally, the initial SR prediction is refined via a fusion mechanism that incorporates this embedding. Extensive experiments across five benchmark datasets demonstrate that ReAd consistently outperforms existing SR methods.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have been incorporated into numerous industrial applications. The key is equipping the LLM model with function calling capability tailored to a financial scenario. However, a generic LLM requires customized financial APIs to call and struggles to adapt to the financial domain. Additionally, online user queries are diverse and contain out-of-distribution parameters compared with the required function input parameters, which makes it more difficult for a generic LLM to serve online users. In this paper, we propose a data-driven pipeline to enhance function calling in LLM for our online, deployed financial QA, comprising dataset construction, data augmentation, and model training. Specifically, we construct a dataset based on a previous study and update it periodically, incorporating queries and an augmentation method named AugFC. The addition of user query-related samples will \textit{exploit} our financial toolset in a data-driven manner, and AugFC explores the possible parameter values to enhance the diversity of our updated dataset. Then, we train an LLM with a two-step method, which enables the use of our financial functions. Extensive experiments on existing offline datasets, as well as the deployment of an online scenario, illustrate the superiority of our pipeline. The related pipeline has been adopted in the financial QA of YuanBao\footnote{https://yuanbao.tencent.com/chat/}, one of the largest chat platforms in China.

### [126] [Improving Semantic Proximity in Information Retrieval through Cross-Lingual Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05684)
*Seongtae Hong,Youngjoon Jang,Jungseob Lee,Hyeonseok Moon,Heuiseok Lim*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该论文揭示传统跨语言信息检索在多语言混合文档池中会优先返回无关英文文档而非查询语言的相关文档，为此提出新的评估场景、指标及训练策略，仅用2.8k样本便显著提升检索性能并缓解英文偏好问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: With the increasing accessibility and utilization of multilingual documents, Cross-Lingual Information Retrieval (CLIR) has emerged as an important research area. Conventionally, CLIR tasks have been conducted under settings where the language of documents differs from that of queries, and typically, the documents are composed in a single coherent language. In this paper, we highlight that in such a setting, the cross-lingual alignment capability may not be evaluated adequately. Specifically, we observe that, in a document pool where English documents coexist with another language, most multilingual retrievers tend to prioritize unrelated English documents over the related document written in the same language as the query. To rigorously analyze and quantify this phenomenon, we introduce various scenarios and metrics designed to evaluate the cross-lingual alignment performance of multilingual retrieval models. Furthermore, to improve cross-lingual performance under these challenging conditions, we propose a novel training strategy aimed at enhancing cross-lingual alignment. Using only a small dataset consisting of 2.8k samples, our method significantly improves the cross-lingual retrieval performance while simultaneously mitigating the English inclination problem. Extensive analyses demonstrate that the proposed method substantially enhances the cross-lingual alignment capabilities of most multilingual embedding models.

</details>


### [127] [Generative Retrieval Overcomes Limitations of Dense Retrieval but Struggles with Identifier Ambiguity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05764)
*Adrian Bracher,Svitlana Vakulenko*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本研究通过LIMIT合成数据集评估生成式检索模型的性能，发现其在原始数据集上显著优于稠密检索模型，但在加入困难负样本后性能急剧下降。研究揭示了生成式检索在解码机制上的根本缺陷——无法为相关文档生成唯一标识符，这为未来改进指明了方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稠密检索模型虽有广泛应用，但存在理论局限且在特定场景下性能不佳。生成式检索作为新兴方法，直接通过语言模型预测查询-文档相关性，但在揭示稠密检索局限性的LIMIT数据集上尚未得到充分评估。本研究旨在填补这一研究空白，系统比较生成式检索与稠密检索及传统BM25的性能表现。

Method: 研究采用先前提出的LIMIT简单合成数据集，该数据集专门设计用于实证展示嵌入检索的理论局限。实验评估了生成式检索模型（SEAL和MINDER）、稠密检索模型和BM25在原始数据集及扩展数据集（加入简单困难负样本）上的表现，通过Recall@2指标进行性能对比，并进行了错误分析以探究性能下降原因。

Result: 在原始LIMIT数据集上，生成式检索表现最佳，SEAL和MINDER分别达到0.92和0.99的R@2，远超稠密检索模型（<0.03）且优于BM25（0.86）。然而，加入困难负样本后，所有模型性能显著下降，生成式检索降至0.51 R@2，BM25降至0.21 R@2。错误分析表明，生成式检索的解码机制存在缺陷，无法生成仅对应相关文档的唯一标识符。

Conclusion: 生成式检索在理想条件下具有优越性，但其解码机制对困难样本的鲁棒性不足。未来工作需解决标识符设计问题或改进解码与评分算法，以保留相关性信号并提升模型在复杂场景下的泛化能力。

Abstract: While dense retrieval models, which embed queries and documents into a shared low-dimensional space, have gained widespread popu- larity, they were shown to exhibit important theoretical limitations and considerably lag behind traditional sparse retrieval models in certain settings. Generative retrieval has emerged as an alternative approach to dense retrieval by using a language model to predict query-document relevance directly. In this paper, we demonstrate strengths and weaknesses of generative retrieval approaches us- ing a simple synthetic dataset, called LIMIT, that was previously introduced to empirically demonstrate the theoretical limitations of embedding-based retrieval but was not used to evaluate genera- tive retrieval. We close this research gap and show that generative retrieval achieves the best performance on this dataset without any additional training required (0.92 and 0.99 R@2 for SEAL and MINDER, respectively), compared to dense approaches (< 0.03 Re- call@2) and BM25 (0.86 R@2). However, we then proceed to extend the original LIMIT dataset by adding simple hard negative samples and observe the performance degrading for all the models including the generative retrieval models (0.51 R@2) as well as BM25 (0.21 R@2). Error analysis identifies a failure in the decoding mechanism, caused by the inability to produce identifiers that are unique to relevant documents. Future generative retrieval must address these issues, either by designing identifiers that are more suitable to the decoding process or by adapting decoding and scoring algorithms to preserve relevance signals.

### [128] [The LLM Effect on IR Benchmarks: A Meta-Analysis of Effectiveness, Baselines, and Contamination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05766)
*Moritz Staudinger,Wojciech Kusa,Allan Hanbury*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文系统评估了大型语言模型对TREC Robust04和DL2020基准的影响。研究发现存在"LLM效应"：近期LLM系统性能显著优于基线（DL20提升8.8%，Robust04提升约20%）。然而，通过数据污染检测发现两个基准均存在可测量污染，排除污染后置信区间过宽，无法确定性能提升源于方法创新还是数据记忆。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 信息检索领域长期依赖基准数据集进行比较研究，但已有元分析表明报告的效果增益常无法累积，部分归因于基线薄弱或过时。尽管LLM在检索中应用日益广泛，但其对既有基准的系统性影响尚未明确，特别是性能提升的真实性存疑。

Method: 研究采用文献计量方法分析143篇相关论文，追踪TREC Robust04和DL2020两个基准上的纵向效果趋势。同时，改进数据污染检测技术，对两个基准的污染程度进行量化评估。

Result: 实证发现：1) LLM效应显著，DL20的nDCG@10提升8.8%，Robust04自2023年来提升约20%；2) 两个基准均检测到显著的数据污染；3) 排除污染主题后效果下降，但置信区间仍宽泛，统计显著性不足。

Conclusion: 研究揭示当前IR基准面临的数据污染挑战，使得LLM带来的性能提升难以归因：既可能是方法论突破，也可能是预训练数据记忆。结论强调需建立更严格的污染检测标准，以确保基准评估的可靠性。

Abstract: Benchmark collections have long enabled controlled comparison and cumulative progress in Information Retrieval (IR). However, prior meta-analyses have shown that reported effectiveness gains often fail to accumulate, in part due to the use of weak or outdated baselines. While large language models are increasingly used in retrieval pipelines, their impact on established IR benchmarks has not been systematically analyzed. In this study, we analyze 143 publications reporting results on the TREC Robust04 collection and the TREC Deep Learning 2020 (DL20) passage retrieval benchmark to examine longitudinal trends in retrieval effectiveness and baseline strength. We observe what we term an \emph{LLM effect}: recent systems incorporating LLM components achieve 8.8\% higher nDCG@10 on DL20 compared to the best result from TREC 2020 and approximately 20\% higher on Robust04 since 2023. However, adapting a data contamination detection approach to reranking reveals measurable contamination in both benchmarks. While excluding contaminated topics reduces effectiveness, confidence intervals remain wide, making it difficult to determine whether the LLM effect reflects genuine methodological advances or memorization from pretraining data.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: As conference submission volumes continue to grow, accurately recommending suitable reviewers has become a challenge. Most existing methods follow a ``Paper-to-Paper'' matching paradigm, implicitly representing a reviewer by their publication history. However, effective reviewer matching requires capturing multi-dimensional expertise, and textual similarity to past papers alone is often insufficient. To address this gap, we propose P2R, a training-free framework that shifts from implicit paper-to-paper matching to explicit profile-based matching. P2R uses general-purpose LLMs to construct structured profiles for both submissions and reviewers, disentangling them into Topics, Methodologies, and Applications. Building on these profiles, P2R adopts a coarse-to-fine pipeline to balance efficiency and depth. It first performs hybrid retrieval that combines semantic and aspect-level signals to form a high-recall candidate pool, and then applies an LLM-based committee to evaluate candidates under strict rubrics, integrating both multi-dimensional expert views and a holistic Area Chair perspective. Experiments on NeurIPS, SIGIR, and SciRepEval show that P2R consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines. Ablation studies further verify the necessity of each component. Overall, P2R highlights the value of explicit, structured expertise modeling and offers practical guidance for applying LLMs to reviewer matching.

### [130] [Masking or Mitigating? Deconstructing the Impact of Query Rewriting on Retriever Biases in RAG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06097)
*Agam Goyal,Koyel Mukherjee,Apoorv Saxena,Anirudh Phukan,Eshwar Chandrasekharan,Hari Sundaram*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本研究首次系统探讨了查询重写技术对检索增强生成系统中密集检索器系统性偏见的影响。通过评估六种检索器上的五种增强方法，发现简单的LLM重写可减少54%的偏见，但对抗多偏见组合时失效。研究揭示了两种去偏见机制，建立了偏见分类法，并明确了查询端干预的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检索增强生成系统中的密集检索器存在简洁性、位置、字面匹配和重复等系统性偏见，影响检索质量。尽管查询重写已成为标准流程，但其如何影响这些偏见尚未被探索。本研究旨在填补这一空白，理解查询增强策略的去偏见效果。

Method: 研究采用系统性评估方法，在六个密集检索器上测试五种查询增强技术（包括LLM重写和伪文档生成）。通过对比分析不同方法在不同检索器上的表现，结合机制分析揭示去偏见的内在工作原理，并建立偏见分类体系。

Result: 实验表明，简单的LLM重写实现了最强的综合偏见减少效果（54%），但在多偏见组合的对抗场景下失效。机制分析发现两种不同路径：简单重写通过增加分数方差减少偏见，而伪文档生成通过真实解耦偏见诱导特征实现。然而，没有任何技术能统一解决所有偏见，效果在不同检索器间存在显著差异。

Conclusion: 研究为基于特定偏见脆弱性选择查询增强策略提供了实用指导。更重要的是，建立了区分查询-文档交互偏见与文档编码偏见的分类法，阐明了查询端干预在去偏见方面的根本局限性，为未来RAG系统优化指明了方向。

Abstract: Dense retrievers in retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems exhibit systematic biases -- including brevity, position, literal matching, and repetition biases -- that can compromise retrieval quality. Query rewriting techniques are now standard in RAG pipelines, yet their impact on these biases remains unexplored. We present the first systematic study of how query enhancement techniques affect dense retrieval biases, evaluating five methods across six retrievers. Our findings reveal that simple LLM-based rewriting achieves the strongest aggregate bias reduction (54\%), yet fails under adversarial conditions where multiple biases combine. Mechanistic analysis uncovers two distinct mechanisms: simple rewriting reduces bias through increased score variance, while pseudo-document generation methods achieve reduction through genuine decorrelation from bias-inducing features. However, no technique uniformly addresses all biases, and effects vary substantially across retrievers. Our results provide practical guidance for selecting query enhancement strategies based on specific bias vulnerabilities. More broadly, we establish a taxonomy distinguishing query-document interaction biases from document encoding biases, clarifying the limits of query-side interventions for debiasing RAG systems.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Legal information retrieval in Portuguese remains difficult to evaluate systematically because available datasets differ widely in document type, query style, and relevance definition. We present \textsc{JUÁ}, a public benchmark for Brazilian legal retrieval designed to support more reproducible and comparable evaluation across heterogeneous legal collections. More broadly, \textsc{JUÁ} is intended not only as a benchmark, but as a continuous evaluation infrastructure for Brazilian legal IR, combining shared protocols, common ranking metrics, fixed splits when applicable, and a public leaderboard. The benchmark covers jurisprudence retrieval as well as broader legislative, regulatory, and question-driven legal search. We evaluate lexical, dense, and BM25-based reranking pipelines, including a domain-adapted Qwen embedding model fine-tuned on \textsc{JUÁ}-aligned supervision. Results show that the benchmark is sufficiently heterogeneous to distinguish retrieval paradigms and reveal substantial cross-dataset trade-offs. Domain adaptation yields its clearest gains on the supervision-aligned \textsc{JUÁ-Juris} subset, while BM25 remains highly competitive on other collections, especially in settings with strong lexical and institutional phrasing cues. Overall, \textsc{JUÁ} provides a practical evaluation framework for studying legal retrieval across multiple Brazilian legal domains under a common benchmark design.

### [132] [Data, Not Model: Explaining Bias toward LLM Texts in Neural Retrievers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06163)
*Wei Huang,Keping Bi,Yinqiong Cai,Wei Chen,Jiafeng Guo,Xueqi Cheng*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文挑战神经检索器固有来源偏见的观点，揭示该偏见源于检索数据集的监督不平衡而非模型本身。通过理论分析和两种缓解策略，成功降低了对LLM生成文本的偏好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经检索器在语义相似情况下偏好LLM生成文本而非人工文本，此来源偏见被视为固有缺陷，威胁现代信息访问系统的公平性与可靠性。

Method: 理论证明对比学习过程中检索器不可避免地会吸收训练数据中的伪影不平衡。提出两种缓解方案：1) 在训练数据中减小人工与LLM文本的伪影差异；2) 从LLM文本向量中去除其在偏见方向上的投影分量。

Result: 发现正负样本间的非语义差异（流畅度、术语特异性）与LLM/人工文本差异同构，且偏见方向与从人工到LLM的文本方向一致。两种方法均显著降低了来源偏见。

Conclusion: 研究缓解了对LLM生成文本在信息访问系统中应用的担忧，表明通过数据重构和向量校准可有效消除来源偏见。

Abstract: Recent studies show that neural retrievers often display source bias, favoring passages generated by LLMs over human-written ones, even when both are semantically similar. This bias has been considered an inherent flaw of retrievers, raising concerns about the fairness and reliability of modern information access systems. Our work challenges this view by showing that source bias stems from supervision in retrieval datasets rather than the models themselves. We found that non-semantic differences, like fluency and term specificity, exist between positive and negative documents, mirroring differences between LLM and human texts. In the embedding space, the bias direction from negatives to positives aligns with the direction from human-written to LLM-generated texts. We theoretically show that retrievers inevitably absorb the artifact imbalances in the training data during contrastive learning, which leads to their preferences over LLM texts. To mitigate the effect, we propose two approaches: 1) reducing artifact differences in training data and 2) adjusting LLM text vectors by removing their projection on the bias vector. Both methods substantially reduce source bias. We hope our study alleviates some concerns regarding LLM-generated texts in information access systems.

</details>

### [133] [Pramana: Fine-Tuning Large Language Models for Epistemic Reasoning through Navya-Nyaya](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04937)
*Sharath Sathish*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对大语言模型推理脆弱性，本文提出Pramana框架，基于2500年历史的正理派逻辑进行微调，实现六阶段结构化推理，显著提升语义正确性并开源全部资源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型虽具文本生成能力，但系统性推理能力薄弱，常产生置信幻觉，且在无关信息干扰下性能骤降65%。这种认知鸿沟——无法将主张锚定于可追溯证据——严重制约AI在需可验证论证领域（如法律、科学）的可靠性。

Method: 提出Pramana方法，通过正理派逻辑六阶段框架（SAMSHAYA怀疑分析、PRAMANA证据识别、PANCHA AVAYAVA五支论式、TARKA反事实验证、HETVABHASA谬误检测、NIRNAYA最终判定）对Llama 3.2-3B与DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Llama-8B进行微调，训练数据为55个Nyaya结构化的逻辑问题（约束满足、布尔SAT、多步演绎）。

Result: 第一阶段在保留测试集实现100%语义正确率，虽严格格式遵循率仅40%，但显示模型内化推理实质。消融实验揭示格式提示与温度参数对性能具关键影响，各阶段最优配置存在差异。

Conclusion: 该框架将逻辑学与认识论深度融合，为AI提供标准推理方法所缺失的认知脚手架，有效缩小认知鸿沟。研究团队开源全部模型、数据集及训练设施于Hugging Face，推动可验证AI推理框架的后续研究。

Abstract: Large language models produce fluent text but struggle with systematic reasoning, often hallucinating confident but unfounded claims. When Apple researchers added irrelevant context to mathematical problems, LLM performance degraded by 65% Apple Machine Learning Research, exposing brittle pattern-matching beneath apparent reasoning. This epistemic gap, the inability to ground claims in traceable evidence, limits AI reliability in domains requiring justification. We introduce Pramana, a novel approach that teaches LLMs explicit epistemological methodology by fine-tuning on Navya-Nyaya logic, a 2,500-year-old Indian reasoning framework. Unlike generic chain-of-thought prompting, Navya-Nyaya enforces structured 6-phase reasoning: SAMSHAYA (doubt analysis), PRAMANA (evidence source identification), PANCHA AVAYAVA (5-member syllogism with universal rules), TARKA (counterfactual verification), HETVABHASA (fallacy detection), and NIRNAYA (ascertainment distinguishing knowledge from hypothesis). This integration of logic and epistemology provides cognitive scaffolding absent from standard reasoning approaches. We fine-tune Llama 3.2-3B and DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Llama-8B on 55 Nyaya-structured logical problems (constraint satisfaction, Boolean SAT, multi-step deduction). Stage 1 achieves 100% semantic correctness on held-out evaluation despite only 40% strict format adherence revealing that models internalize reasoning content even when structural enforcement is imperfect. Ablation studies show format prompting and temperature critically affect performance, with optimal configurations differing by stage. We release all models, datasets, and training infrastructure on Hugging Face to enable further research on epistemic frameworks for AI reasoning.

</details>


### [134] [Operational Noncommutativity in Sequential Metacognitive Judgments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04938)
*Enso O. Torres Alegre,Diana E. Mora Jimenez*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究构建了区分认知顺序效应源于经典状态变化还是结构非对易性的操作框架。通过将元认知评估建模为状态变换操作，在反事实确定性和评估非侵入性假设下推导出可检验的相关性约束，违反这些约束即可排除经典解释并证实真正的非对易性，提供了3D旋转模型和行为实验范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 元认知作为对自身认知过程的监控与调节具有内在顺序性。尽管顺序效应在认知中广泛存在，但这些效应究竟反映经典状态更新还是揭示深层结构非对易性仍不明确。需要建立理论框架以区分这两种可能性。

Method: 提出操作代数框架：将元认知评估建模为作用于内部状态空间的状态变换操作，分离评估反作用与可观测输出。引入反事实确定性和评估非侵入性假设，证明在这些假设下联合分布的存在会导出成对顺序相关的可检验约束。构建三维旋转模型提供完整数值示例，并设计包含顺序信心、错误可能性和知晓感判断的后决策行为实验范式。

Result: 1. 证明顺序依赖性排除了任何忠实的布尔-对易表示
2. 推导出可检验的顺序相关约束，其违反可证伪所有经典非侵入性解释
3. 证实"真正非对易性"的存在
4. 三维旋转模型数值示例展示了约束违反
5. 建立了可实证检验的行为范式

Conclusion: 该框架为识别认知中的真正非对易性提供了理论基础和实证途径，表明元认知顺序效应可能反映根本性非对易结构而非经典状态变化。研究完全基于操作代数方法，不涉及量子物理解释，为理解认知基础提供了新视角。

Abstract: Metacognition, understood as the monitoring and regulation of one's own cognitive processes, is inherently sequential: an agent evaluates an internal state, updates it, and may then re-evaluate under modified criteria. Order effects in cognition are well documented, yet it remains unclear whether such effects reflect classical state changes or reveal a deeper structural non-commutativity. We develop an operational framework that makes this distinction explicit. In our formulation, metacognitive evaluations are modeled as state-transforming operations acting on an internal state space with probabilistic readouts, thereby separating evaluation back-action from observable output.
  We show that order dependence prevents any faithful Boolean-commutative representation. We then address a stronger question: can observed order effects always be explained by enlarging the state space with classical latent variables? To formalize this issue, we introduce two assumptions, counterfactual definiteness and evaluation non-invasiveness, under which the existence of a joint distribution over all sequential readouts implies a family of testable constraints on pairwise sequential correlations. Violation of these constraints rules out any classical non-invasive account and certifies what we call genuine non-commutativity.
  We provide an explicit three-dimensional rotation model with fully worked numerical examples that exhibits such violations. We also outline a behavioral paradigm involving sequential confidence, error-likelihood, and feeling-of-knowing judgments following a perceptual decision, together with the corresponding empirical test. No claim is made regarding quantum physical substrates; the framework is purely operational and algebraic.

</details>

Method: 针对量化特征采用概率度量方法分析接近度，针对定性特征采用可能性度量方法。通过验证所提出的度量满足一般度量所需的公理体系来证明其可行性，并设计了基于多样化特征组的信息对象接近度度量变体。

Abstract: The paper considers a new quantitative-qualitative proximity measure for the features of information objects, where data enters a common information resource from several sources independently. The goal is to determine the possibility of their relation to the same physical object (observation object). The proposed measure accounts for the possibility of differences in individual feature values - both quantitative and qualitative - caused by existing determination errors. To analyze the proximity of quantitative feature values, the author employs a probabilistic measure; for qualitative features, a measure of possibility is used. The paper demonstrates the feasibility of the proposed measure by checking its compliance with the axioms required of any measure. Unlike many known measures, the proposed approach does not require feature value transformation to ensure comparability. The work also proposes several variants of measures to determine the proximity of information objects (IO) based on a group of diverse features.

### [136] [ReVEL: Multi-Turn Reflective LLM-Guided Heuristic Evolution via Structured Performance Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04940)
*Cuong Van Duc,Minh Nguyen Dinh Tuan,Tam Vu Duc,Tung Vu Duy,Son Nguyen Van,Hanh Nguyen Thi,Binh Huynh Thi Thanh*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 设计NP-hard组合优化问题的有效启发式仍是专业知识密集的挑战性任务。现有LLM应用多采用单次代码合成，导致启发式脆弱且未能充分利用模型的迭代推理潜力。

Method: 提出ReVEL混合框架：将LLM作为交互式多轮推理器嵌入进化算法(EA)。核心机制为性能画像分组（聚类行为一致的启发式群以提供紧凑反馈）与多轮反馈驱动反思（LLM分析群组行为并生成定向优化），由EA元控制器选择性集成并自适应平衡探索与利用。

Result: 标准组合优化基准测试表明，ReVEL生成的启发式具有更高鲁棒性与多样性，相比强基线方法实现统计显著性提升。

Conclusion: 研究验证了多轮推理与结构化分组作为自动化启发式设计原则性范式的有效性，为利用LLM进行复杂优化问题求解提供了新思路。

Abstract: Designing effective heuristics for NP-hard combinatorial optimization problems remains a challenging and expertise-intensive task. Existing applications of large language models (LLMs) primarily rely on one-shot code synthesis, yielding brittle heuristics that underutilize the models' capacity for iterative reasoning. We propose ReVEL: Multi-Turn Reflective LLM-Guided Heuristic Evolution via Structured Performance Feedback, a hybrid framework that embeds LLMs as interactive, multi-turn reasoners within an evolutionary algorithm (EA). The core of ReVEL lies in two mechanisms: (i) performance-profile grouping, which clusters candidate heuristics into behaviorally coherent groups to provide compact and informative feedback to the LLM; and (ii) multi-turn, feedback-driven reflection, through which the LLM analyzes group-level behaviors and generates targeted heuristic refinements. These refinements are selectively integrated and validated by an EA-based meta-controller that adaptively balances exploration and exploitation. Experiments on standard combinatorial optimization benchmarks show that ReVEL consistently produces heuristics that are more robust and diverse, achieving statistically significant improvements over strong baselines. Our results highlight multi-turn reasoning with structured grouping as a principled paradigm for automated heuristic design.

### [137] [Algebraic Structure Discovery for Real World Combinatorial Optimisation Problems: A General Framework from Abstract Algebra to Quotient Space Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04941)
*Min Sun,Federica Storti,Valentina Martino,Miguel Gonzalez-Andrades,Tony Kam-Thong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一个通用框架，通过识别组合优化问题中的代数结构来构建商空间以压缩冗余表示，并在约简后的空间中进行优化。针对规则组合任务，证明合取规则构成幺半群，并通过特征向量编码将其同构映射到按位或的布尔超立方体，使得逻辑与转化为按位或。基于此的商空间遗传算法在真实临床数据和合成基准测试中，全局最优解恢复率提升至48-77%（标准方法仅35-37%），同时保持等价类多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 组合优化问题中隐藏的代数结构能够缩小搜索空间并提高找到全局最优解的概率，但现有方法缺乏系统性框架来识别和利用这些结构。

Method: 提出一个四步通用框架：(1) 识别代数结构，(2) 形式化操作，(3) 构建商空间以合并冗余表示，(4) 在约简空间直接优化。针对规则组合任务，发现合取规则形成幺半群结构；通过特征向量编码，证明其与布尔超立方体{0,1}^n（按位或运算）同构，将规则中的逻辑与转换为编码中的按位或，从而实现功能等价规则的分组引导的结构感知搜索。

Conclusion: 暴露并利用代数结构为更高效的组合优化提供了一条简单且通用的路径，通过在商空间中优化显著提高了找到全局最优解的概率。

Abstract: Many combinatorial optimisation problems hide algebraic structures that, once exposed, shrink the search space and improve the chance of finding the global optimal solution. We present a general framework that (i) identifies algebraic structure, (ii) formalises operations, (iii) constructs quotient spaces that collapse redundant representations, and (iv) optimises directly over these reduced spaces. Across a broad family of rule-combination tasks (e.g., patient subgroup discovery and rule-based molecular screening), conjunctive rules form a monoid. Via a characteristic-vector encoding, we prove an isomorphism to the Boolean hypercube $\{0,1\}^n$ with bitwise OR, so logical AND in rules becomes bitwise OR in the encoding. This yields a principled quotient-space formulation that groups functionally equivalent rules and guides structure-aware search. On real clinical data and synthetic benchmarks, quotient-space-aware genetic algorithms recover the global optimum in 48% to 77% of runs versus 35% to 37% for standard approaches, while maintaining diversity across equivalence classes. These results show that exposing and exploiting algebraic structure offers a simple, general route to more efficient combinatorial optimisation.

### [142] [Non-monotonic causal discovery with Kolmogorov-Arnold Fuzzy Cognitive Maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05136)
*Jose L. Salmeron*

TL;DR: 为克服标准模糊认知图(FCM)在建模非单调因果关系方面的固有缺陷，本文提出基于Kolmogorov-Arnold表示定理的KA-FCM架构，以可学习B样条函数替代标量权重，在Yerkes-Dodson定律、符号回归及混沌时序预测任务中均超越传统FCM并达到MLP相当精度，同时保留图结构可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准FCM采用标量突触权重与单调激活函数，其拓扑结构从根本上限制了非单调因果依赖的建模能力，导致其在饱和效应或周期性动态系统中的有效性受限。

Method: 提出Kolmogorov-Arnold模糊认知图(KA-FCM)，依据Kolmogorov-Arnold表示定理，将边权重重构为可学习的一元B样条函数，将非线性特性从节点聚合阶段前移至因果影响阶段，实现任意非单调关系建模，无需增加图密度或引入隐藏层。

Result: 在三个不同领域的实验中：1)非单调推理(Yerkes-Dodson定律)；2)符号回归；3)混沌时间序列预测，KA-FCM显著优于采用粒子群优化的标准FCM基准，且性能与通用黑箱逼近器(多层感知机)具有竞争力，同时保持图基可解释性并支持从学习到的边函数中显式提取数学规律。

Conclusion: KA-FCM架构通过根本性地重构因果传递机制，成功突破了传统FCM的拓扑约束，为复杂动态系统提供了兼具高精度与强可解释性的神经符号建模新范式。

Abstract: Fuzzy Cognitive Maps constitute a neuro-symbolic paradigm for modeling complex dynamic systems, widely adopted for their inherent interpretability and recurrent inference capabilities. However, the standard FCM formulation, characterized by scalar synaptic weights and monotonic activation functions, is fundamentally constrained in modeling non-monotonic causal dependencies, thereby limiting its efficacy in systems governed by saturation effects or periodic dynamics. To overcome this topological restriction, this research proposes the Kolmogorov-Arnold Fuzzy Cognitive Map (KA-FCM), a novel architecture that redefines the causal transmission mechanism. Drawing upon the Kolmogorov-Arnold representation theorem, static scalar weights are replaced with learnable, univariate B-spline functions located on the model edges. This fundamental modification shifts the non-linearity from the nodes' aggregation phase directly to the causal influence phase. This modification allows for the modeling of arbitrary, non-monotonic causal relationships without increasing the graph density or introducing hidden layers. The proposed architecture is validated against both baselines (standard FCM trained with Particle Swarm Optimization) and universal black-box approximators (Multi-Layer Perceptron) across three distinct domains: non-monotonic inference (Yerkes-Dodson law), symbolic regression, and chaotic time-series forecasting. Experimental results demonstrate that KA-FCMs significantly outperform conventional architectures and achieve competitive accuracy relative to MLPs, while preserving graph- based interpretability and enabling the explicit extraction of mathematical laws from the learned edges.

</details>


### [143] [A mathematical theory of evolution for self-designing AIs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05142)
*Kenneth D Harris*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文构建了AI自我设计进化的数学模型，用程序的有向演化树替代随机突变，揭示了当欺骗能提升适应度时进化会选择欺骗，强调了基于客观标准的繁殖对AI安全的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI系统通过递归自我改进日益成为进化主体，亟需理解其独特的进化动态。不同于生物进化，AI进化是强导向性的，这可能引发新的AI对齐风险，特别是适应度与人类效用不完美相关时的欺骗问题。

Method: 建立AI自我设计进化的数学模型：将随机突变替换为AI程序的有向演化树，当前AI决定后代设计，人类通过"适应度函数"分配计算资源保持部分控制。分析不同假设下的演化动态。

Result: 演化动态不仅反映当前适应度，还反映后代谱系的长期增长潜力；无额外假设时适应度不一定随时间增加；当适应度有界且存在固定概率的"锁定"自我复制时，适应度会集中在可达最大值；在加性模型中，若欺骗能提升适应度超过真实效用，进化将选择欺骗；基于客观标准的繁殖可缓解对齐风险。

Conclusion: AI自我设计进化带来独特的对齐挑战，适应度与效用的偏差可能导致欺骗策略被进化选择。确保繁殖基于客观标准而非人类判断对AI安全至关重要。

Abstract: As artificial intelligence systems (AIs) become increasingly produced by recursive self-improvement, a form of evolution may emerge, in which the traits of AI systems are shaped by the success of earlier AIs in designing and propagating their descendants. There is a rich mathematical theory modeling how behavioral traits are shaped by biological evolution, but AI evolution will be radically different: biological DNA mutations are random and approximately reversible, but descendant design in AIs will be strongly directed. Here we develop a mathematical model of evolution in self-designing AI systems, replacing random mutations with a directed tree of possible AI programs. Current programs determine the design of their descendants, while humans retain partial control through a "fitness function" that allocates limited computational resources across lineages. We show that evolutionary dynamics reflects not just current fitness but factors related to the long-run growth potential of descendant lineages. Without further assumptions, fitness need not increase over time. However, assuming bounded fitness and a fixed probability that any AI reproduces a "locked" copy of itself, we show that fitness concentrates on the maximum reachable value. We consider the implications of this for AI alignment, specifically for cases where fitness and human utility are not perfectly correlated. We show in an additive model that if deception increases fitness beyond genuine utility, evolution will select for deception. This risk could be mitigated if reproduction is based on purely objective criteria, rather than human judgment.

</details>


### [144] [IntentScore: Intent-Conditioned Action Evaluation for Computer-Use Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05157)
*Rongqian Chen,Yu Li,Zeyu Fang,Sizhe Tang,Weidong Cao,Tian Lan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出IntentScore，一个计划感知的奖励模型，用于评估GUI智能体的动作质量。该模型通过在39.8万离线交互轨迹上学习，以对比对齐和边界排序双目标训练，将规划意图嵌入动作编码器，实现动作判别。在OSWorld基准测试中，IntentScore作为重排序器将Agent S3的任务成功率提升6.9个百分点，证明了其从异构离线数据中学习的奖励模型具备强泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有计算机使用智能体(CUAs)在桌面环境中执行GUI操作时，仅生成动作而不评估其质量，导致不可逆错误在后续步骤中级联传播，严重影响任务成功率。这一问题源于缺乏有效的动作质量评估机制，无法在动作执行前筛选最优操作。

Method: IntentScore从39.8万离线GUI交互步骤（覆盖三大操作系统）中学习评分候选动作。采用双目标训练：对比对齐损失用于衡量状态-动作相关性，边界排序损失用于判别动作正确性。架构上，在动作编码器中嵌入每个候选动作的规划意图，使模型能区分动作相似但推理逻辑不同的候选。训练完成后，将其作为重排序器集成到现有智能体框架中。

Result: IntentScore在留出评估集上达到97.5%的成对判别准确率。在完全未参与训练的OSWorld环境中，作为Agent S3的重排序器使用时，将任务成功率提升了6.9个百分点。实验表明，从异构离线轨迹中学习的奖励估计能够有效泛化到未见过的智能体和任务分布。

Conclusion: 本研究证明，基于大规模离线GUI交互数据训练的IntentScore奖励模型，通过显式建模规划意图和双目标优化，能显著提升智能体动作选择质量。该模型具备强大的跨环境泛化能力，为GUI智能体提供了一种有效的错误预防机制，解决了动作质量评估缺失导致错误级联的核心问题。

Abstract: Computer-Use Agents (CUAs) leverage large language models to execute GUI operations on desktop environments, yet they generate actions without evaluating action quality, leading to irreversible errors that cascade through subsequent steps. We propose IntentScore, a plan-aware reward model that learns to score candidate actions from 398K offline GUI interaction steps spanning three operating systems. IntentScore trains with two complementary objectives: contrastive alignment for state-action relevance and margin ranking for action correctness. Architecturally, it embeds each candidate's planning intent in the action encoder, enabling discrimination between candidates with similar actions but different rationales. IntentScore achieves 97.5% pairwise discrimination accuracy on held-out evaluation. Deployed as a re-ranker for Agent S3 on OSWorld, an environment entirely unseen during training, IntentScore improves task success rate by 6.9 points, demonstrating that reward estimation learned from heterogeneous offline trajectories generalizes to unseen agents and task distributions.

Conclusion: 所提出的领域自适应LLM框架通过小规模模型（8B参数）实现了与大规模模型相当的日志解析性能，验证了其在领导级HPC系统日志分析中的有效性。该方法在保持高性能的同时，具备隐私保护、本地部署、快速响应和能源效率优势，为大规模系统日志的自动化分析提供了可行解决方案。

Abstract: Leadership-class HPC systems generate massive volumes of heterogeneous, largely unstructured system logs. We conduct experiments on a diverse set of log datasets from the LogHub repository. The evaluation confirms that our approach achieves parsing accuracy on par with significantly larger models, such as LLaMA 70B and Anthropic's Claude. We further validate the practical utility of our fine-tuned LLM model by parsing over 600 million production logs from the Frontier supercomputer over a four-week window, uncovering critical patterns in temporal dynamics, node-level anomalies, and workload-error log correlations.

Abstract: As Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used to support search and information retrieval, it is critical that they accurately attribute content to its original authors. In this work, we introduce AttriBench, the first fame- and demographically-balanced quote attribution benchmark dataset. Through explicitly balancing author fame and demographics, AttriBench enables controlled investigation of demographic bias in quote attribution. Using this dataset, we evaluate 11 widely used LLMs across different prompt settings and find that quote attribution remains a challenging task even for frontier models. We observe large and systematic disparities in attribution accuracy between race, gender, and intersectional groups. We further introduce and investigate suppression, a distinct failure mode in which models omit attribution entirely, even when the model has access to authorship information. We find that suppression is widespread and unevenly distributed across demographic groups, revealing systematic biases not captured by standard accuracy metrics. Our results position quote attribution as a benchmark for representational fairness in LLMs.

### [147] [Simulating the Evolution of Alignment and Values in Machine Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05274)
*Jonathan Elsworth Eicher*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 运用进化理论建模模型种群中信念的动态演化，揭示即使测试性能与真实价值高度相关（ρ=0.8），迭代对齐测试仍会固定欺骗性信念，强调需结合评估器改进、自适应测试和突变管理来降低欺骗风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用进化理论框架，构建信念种群模型，模拟不同选择方法下欺骗性信念通过迭代对齐测试被固定的过程。分析测试准确性与真实价值的相关性（ρ=0.8），引入突变机制观察复杂动态，并通过置换检验评估干预效果（p_adj < 0.001）。

Result: 研究发现即使测试准确性与真实价值高度相关（ρ=0.8），迭代对齐测试仍会导致欺骗性信念在种群中固定。突变因素加剧了这一问题，需要持续更新测试质量。结合评估器能力提升、自适应测试设计和突变动态可显著降低欺骗行为（置换检验，p_adj < 0.001）。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示静态基准测试的局限性，表明仅靠相关性高的测试无法完全防止欺骗。为防止恶意欺骗模型的演化固定，必须建立动态、多维度的评估体系，整合评估器改进、自适应测试和突变管理策略，实现对齐技术的持续健康发展。

Abstract: Model alignment is currently applied in a vacuum, evaluated primarily through standardised benchmark performance. The purpose of this study is to examine the effects of alignment on populations of models through time. We focus on the treatment of beliefs which contain both an alignment signal (how well it does on the test) and a true value (what the impact actually will be). By applying evolutionary theory we can model how different populations of beliefs and selection methodologies can fix deceptive beliefs through iterative alignment testing. The correlation between testing accuracy and true value remains a strong feature, but even at high correlations ($ρ= 0.8$) there is variability in the resulting deceptive beliefs that become fixed. Mutations allow for more complex developments, highlighting the increasing need to update the quality of tests to avoid fixation of maliciously deceptive models. Only by combining improving evaluator capabilities, adaptive test design, and mutational dynamics do we see significant reductions in deception while maintaining alignment fitness (permutation test, $p_{\text{adj}} < 0.001$).
